\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ include\ functionality\ removed\ from\ the\ core\ profile,\ such\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ fixed-\/function\ vertex\ and\ fragment\ processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It\ is\ not\ possible\ to\ \#include\ both\ <GL/glcorearb.h>\ and\ either\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ <GL/gl.h>\ or\ <GL/glext.h>\ in\ the\ same\ source\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
